<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">&#151;How To Vote&#151; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Please Choose One of the Following Voting Methods </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Vote In Person: The proxy materials described above contain a map showing the location of the Meeting and information
regarding admittance requirements for the Meeting and voting in person. At the Meeting, you will need to request a ballot to vote these shares. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Vote By Internet: To vote now by Internet, go to www.proxyvote.com. Have the information that is printed in the box marked
by the arrow 1234 5678 9012 (located on the following page) available and follow the instructions. You can also sign up for electronic delivery of future proxy materials by following the prompts after voting. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Vote By Mail or By Phone: You can vote by mail by requesting a paper copy of the materials, which will include a proxy
card. The proxy card will include instructions for voting by phone. Instructions for voting by phone are also on page 5 of the proxy statement, which you can view online as described above. </FONT></P>
